,MTHONG NAS NYON MONGS RNAMS KYANG BSHIG ,THIBS PO'I DPE RNAMS
RAB SPANGS TE, ,DE DAG 'PHAGS

PA'I SPYOD YUL DONG, ,SHES DANG SHES BYA'I BYE BRAG GIS, ,DE
GNYIS GZHAN DU MI BRTAG PA, ,BLO NGAN RNAMS KYIS MI RTOGS TE,
,BRJOD DU MED PAR SMRA BAR BYED, ,JI LTAR TZANDAN

BYAS PA'I RNGA, ,BYIS PA DAG NI GZHAN DU BYED, ,DE BZHIN TZANDAN
AA GAR 'DRA'I, ,SHES PA RTOG GE NGAN PAS SO, ,LANGS NAS KHA BAS
PHYIS MI LEN, ,LHUNG BZED GNAS DANG PHYIR


@306A *, ,BA CAN, ,GDONG 'GYUR LA SOGS NYES PA RNAMS, ,DAG PAS
ZAS LA SPYAD PAR BYA, ,SU ZHIG TSUL 'DI RIGS PAS DPOG BYED PA,
,DAD LDAN

RNAL 'BYOR BRTZON ZHING MI RTOG PA, ,MI GNAS DON LA RTEN PAR GYUR
PA DE, ,CHOS KYI RNAM PAR GSER BZHIN SPYAD PAR BYA, ,BLUN PAS
SRID DANG MI SRID RKYEN RTOG PA, ,DE NI LTA NGAN

DRA BA DRI MAR BCAS, ,'DOD CHAGS ZHE SDANG GTI MUG BCAS PA LDOG
,CHAGS MED SANGS RGYAS PHYAG GIS DBANG BSKUR 'GYUR, ,MU STEGS
RGYU YI PHYOGS KYIS BSLAD, ,

GZHAN YANG RKYEN GYIS RNAM PAR RMONGS, ,GZHAN DAG RGYU MED DE
'BYUNG BAS, ,DON MED PA NI CHAD PA'O, ,YID DANG RNAM PAR SHES PA
DANG, ,RNAM PAR SMIN PA GYUR PA STE, ,YID

NI KUN GZHI LAS BYUNG BA, ,RNAM PAR SHES PA YID LAS BYUNG, ,KUN
GZHI LAS NI SEMS KUN KYANG, ,DBA' RLABS BZHIN DU 'BYUNG BAR
'GYUR, ,THAMS CAD BAG CHAGS

RGYU LAS BYUNG, ,RKYEN BZHIN DU NI 'BYUNG BA'O, ,SKAD CIG THA DAD
'BREL BAS SBREL, ,RANG GI SEMS NI DON LA 'DZIN, ,DBYIBS KYI MTSAN
NYID RNAM PAR DAG ,YID DANG MIG

LA SOGS LAS BYUNG, ,THOG MA MED NAS RNAM PAR 'BREL, ,DON SNANG
BAG CHAGS RNAMS LAS BYUNG, ,JI LTAR SNANG BA SEMS SNANG STE, ,MU
STEGS LTA BA BZLOG PA YI, ,DE YI


@306B RGYUS BYUNG GZHAN NYID KYANG, ,DE LA DMIGS NAS 'JUG PAR
'GYUR, ,DE LAS LTA BA SHES PA DAG ,'KHOR BAR RAB TU 'JUG PAR
'GYUR, ,DNGOS PO RMI LAM SGYU MA 'DRA, ,DRI ZA'I GRONG

KHYER RNAMS BZHIN TE, ,SMIG RGYU BA DANG CHU ZLA LTAR, ,RANG GI
RNAM RTOG RNAM PAR BSGOMS, ,'JUG PA'I RNAM PAS DE BZHIN NYID,
,YANG DAG YE SHES DE YI GNAS, ,SGYU MA DPA'

BAR 'GRO LA SOGS, ,TING NGE 'DZIN NI GZHAN RNAMS DANG, ,MNGON PAR
SHES DANG DBANG RNAMS DANG, ,YE SHES SGYU MA LTA BU DANG, ,DE
BZHIN GSHEGS PAS DBANG BSKUR BA, ,

SA LA ZHUGS NAS THOB PAR 'GYUR, ,GANG TSE 'GRO BA RNAM RTOG
MTHONG, ,DE TSE SEMS NI LDOG PAR 'GYUR, ,SA NI RAB TU DGA' BA
DANG, ,SANGS RGYAS SA DANG SA RNAMS 'THOB, ,

GNAS NI RAB TU GYUR PA'I PHYIR, ,JI LTAR SNA TSOGS NOR BU BZHIN,
,SEMS CAN RNAMS KYI DON BYED DE, ,CHU LA GZUGS BRNYAN JI BZHIN
NO, ,YOD DANG MED PA'I PHYOGS RNAMS

DANG; ;GNYIS DANG GNYIS MED PA DANG BRAL, ,NYAN THOS RANG RGYAL
'DAS GYUR NA, ,SA BDUN PAR NI 'GYUR BA YIN, ,SO SO RANG CHOS
MTHONG BAS NI, ,YANG DAG PA YIS

SBYANGS TE, ,PHYI ROL MU STEGS RNAMS SPANGS PA'I, ,THEG PA CHEN
PO BSHAD PAR BYA, ,RNAM PAR RTOG PAR RAB GYUR NA, ,SHI 'PHOS 'JIG
PA RNAMS SPANGS PA, ,RI BONG SPU YI


@307A *, ,NOR BU BZHIN, ,GROL BA RNAMS LA TSUL YANG BSHAD, ,JI
LTAR TSIG LA TSIG GNAS PA, ,GAL TE RIGS LA RIGS DE BZHIN, ,DE
PHYIR RIGS PA'I

RIGS PA YIN, ,DE LAS GZHAN DU MA RTOG CIG ,MIG DANG LAS DANG SRED
PA DANG, ,MA RIG DE BZHIN TSUL BZHIN MIN, ,MIG DANG GZUGS DANG
YID RNAMS DANG, ,RNYOG PA'I

YID KYANG DE BZHIN NO, ,'PHAGS PA LANGKAR GSHEGS PA ZHES BYA BA
THEG PA CHEN PO'I MDO JI SNYED PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,BCOM LDAN 'DAS
KYI RING LUGS PA, 'GOS

CHOS GRUB KYIS RGYA'I DPE LAS BSGYUR TE GTAN LA PHAB PA'O,,
